                    DARLA_CONFIG.onFinishParse = function(eventId, result) {

                            i, l, position, posObj, mutexPos, posName, container, display,
                            re = /([A-Z0-9]+)(-[0-9]+)*/;
                    
                        for (i = 0, l = ps.length; i < l; i++) {
                            position = ps[i];
                            posObj = result.item(position);
                            if (!posObj || posObj.hasErr) {
                                noads.push(position);
                            }
                        }

                        // handle mutual exclusion for client side fetched ads
                        if (eventId === LB_EVENT || eventId === AUTO_EVENT) {
                            for (position in MUTEX_ADS) {
                                if (MUTEX_ADS.hasOwnProperty(position) && ps.indexOf(position) >= 0 && noads.indexOf(position) === -1) {
                                    for (i = 0, l = MUTEX_ADS[position].length; i < l; i++) {
                                        mutexPos = MUTEX_ADS[position][i];
                                        if (ps.indexOf(mutexPos) >= 0 && noads.indexOf(mutexPos) === -1) {
                                            noads.push(mutexPos);
                                        }
                                    }
                                }
                            }
                            for (i = 0, l = ps.length; i < l; i++) {
                                position = ps[i];
                                posName = re.exec(position)[1];
                                container = Y.one('.yom-ad-'+posName);
                                if (container) {
                                    display = container.getStyle('display');
                                    if (display === 'none' && noads.indexOf(position) === -1) {
                                        container.show();
                                    } else if (display !== 'none' && noads.indexOf(position) >= 0) {
                                        container.hide();
                                    }
                                }
                            }

                            } else {
                                Y.log('LDRB is noad or size is 1x1', 'info', 'darla');
                            }

                        return {
                            _prepareNodes: function() {
                                for(var cleanId in nodes){
                                    var center = Y.one("#"+cleanId+" > center");
                                    if(center != null && center && !Y.one("#" + nodes[cleanId].id)){
                                        center.set("innerHTML","");
                                        center.insert(nodes[cleanId].node);
                                    }
                                }
                            }

                    })();

                    /* setting up DARLA events */
                    var w = window,
                        D = w.DARLA,
                        C = w.DARLA_CONFIG,
                        DM = w.DOC_DOMAIN_SET || 0;
                    if (D) {
                        if (D && C) {
                            C.dm = DM;
                        }
                        
                        DARLA_CONFIG.nodeMgr._prepareNodes();
                        
                        /* setting DARLA configuration */
                        DARLA.config(C);

                        /* prefetch Ads if applicable */
                        DARLA.prefetched("fc");

                        /* rendering prefetched Ad */
                        DARLA.render();  
                    }

                    return {
                        event: function (eventId, spaceId, adsSa) {
                            if (window.DARLA && eventId) {
                                DARLA_CONFIG.nodeMgr._prepareNodes();
                                var eventConfig = {};
                                if (!isNaN(spaceId)) {
                                    eventConfig.sp = spaceId;
                                }
                                /* Site attributes */
                                adsSa = (typeof adsSa !== "undefined" && adsSa !== null) ? adsSa : "";
                                eventConfig.sa = DARLA_CONFIG.events[eventId].sa_orig.replace ? DARLA_CONFIG.events[eventId].sa_orig.replace("ADSSA", adsSa) : "";
                                DARLA.event(eventId, eventConfig);
                            }
                        },
                        render: function() {
                            if (!!(Y.one('#yom-slideshow-lightbox') || Y.one('#content-lightbox') || false)) {
                                /* skip configuring DARLA in case of lightbox being triggered */
                            } else {
                                // abort current darla action
                                if (DARLA && DARLA.abort) {
                                    DARLA.abort();
                                }

                                /* prepare node is mainly for injected ad, eg. LREC within story body */
                                DARLA_CONFIG.nodeMgr._prepareNodes();

                                /* setting DARLA configuration */
                                DARLA.config(DARLA_CONFIG);

                                /* prefetch Ads if applicable */
                                DARLA.prefetched("fc");

                                /* rendering prefetched Ad */
                                DARLA.render();  
                            }
                        }
                    };

                })(); /* End of YUI.AdsDarla */

            <div id="c4-shelves-container" class=""> 
             <div class="compact-shelf shelf-item yt-uix-shelfslider yt-uix-shelfslider-at-head yt-uix-shelfslider-at-tail vve-check clearfix branded-page-box yt-section-hover-container fluid-shelf yt-uix-tdl" data-sessionlink="ei=qZMfU6mQCsOn-AP89YHoAg&amp;ved=CB4Q3BwoAA"> 
              <h2 class="branded-page-module-title"> <a href="/playlist?list=PLA9178DCDD20FFD85" class="yt-uix-sessionlink branded-page-module-title-link spf-nolink" data-sessionlink="ei=qZMfU6mQCsOn-AP89YHoAg"> <span class="branded-page-module-title-text"> <span class="">Culver Center of the Arts | Uncovered II</span> </span> </a> <a href="/watch?v=P8kGevv7jVg&amp;list=PLA9178DCDD20FFD85" class="yt-uix-button  shelves-play yt-uix-sessionlink yt-uix-button-default yt-uix-button-size-small" data-sessionlink="ei=qZMfU6mQCsOn-AP89YHoAg"><span class="yt-uix-button-icon-wrapper"><img class="yt-uix-button-icon yt-uix-button-icon-play-all" src="http://s.ytimg.com/yts/img/pixel-vfl3z5WfW.gif" alt="" title="" /></span><span class="yt-uix-button-content">Play </span></a> </h2> 
              <div class="shelf-description yt-ui-ellipsis yt-ui-ellipsis-2">
                Learn more about performances at http://www.culvercenter.ucr.edu/performances/
               <br />
               <br />Uncovered II: Socially-Conscious Artists: Through the use of the Tableau Vivant, dance and music, life-size versions of some of hip hop's most politically charged and message-conscious album covers will be brought to life. From the politically charged Public Enemy challenging the structure of not only American society but of the world, to Lauren Hill's compelling presence bringing a different form of female representation to hip hop music, to OutKast's outlandish and innovative style, the focus of the second version of Uncovered is albums and artists who left a powerful mark on hip hop as well as American culture through their provocative, fearless and visionary music. 
              </div>

             <div class="compact-shelf shelf-item yt-uix-shelfslider yt-uix-shelfslider-at-head yt-uix-shelfslider-at-tail vve-check clearfix branded-page-box yt-section-hover-container fluid-shelf yt-uix-tdl" data-sessionlink="ei=qZMfU6mQCsOn-AP89YHoAg&amp;ved=CDcQ3BwoAQ"> 
              <h2 class="branded-page-module-title"> <a href="/playlist?list=PLB86872AFCE43E54E" class="yt-uix-sessionlink branded-page-module-title-link spf-nolink" data-sessionlink="ei=qZMfU6mQCsOn-AP89YHoAg"> <span class="branded-page-module-title-text"> <span class="">The Great Picture</span> </span> </a> <a href="/watch?v=wF_g0ZY2AnM&amp;list=PLB86872AFCE43E54E" class="yt-uix-button  shelves-play yt-uix-sessionlink yt-uix-button-default yt-uix-button-size-small" data-sessionlink="ei=qZMfU6mQCsOn-AP89YHoAg"><span class="yt-uix-button-icon-wrapper"><img class="yt-uix-button-icon yt-uix-button-icon-play-all" src="http://s.ytimg.com/yts/img/pixel-vfl3z5WfW.gif" alt="" title="" /></span><span class="yt-uix-button-content">Play </span></a> </h2> 
              <div class="shelf-description yt-ui-ellipsis yt-ui-ellipsis-2">
                Learn more about THE GREAT PICTURE at http://sweeney.ucr.edu/exhibitions/the-great-picture/
               <br />
               <br />UCR Sweeney Art Gallery &amp; Culver Center of the Arts present The Great Picture: The World's Largest Photograph &amp; The Legacy Project, an exhibition in three parts that tells the tale of the successful campaign to make the world's largest camera and photograph. The photo's mammoth scale of 32 x 111 feet earned it a place in Guinness World Records, and made it a photo history landmark. 
              </div>

              <h2 class="branded-page-module-title"> <a href="/playlist?list=PL677E3761E7486830" class="yt-uix-sessionlink branded-page-module-title-link spf-nolink" data-sessionlink="ei=qZMfU6mQCsOn-AP89YHoAg"> <span class="branded-page-module-title-text"> <span class="">Culver Center of the Arts | Gala Reception</span> </span> </a> <a href="/watch?v=szHfxbWJyro&amp;list=PL677E3761E7486830" class="yt-uix-button  shelves-play yt-uix-sessionlink yt-uix-button-default yt-uix-button-size-small" data-sessionlink="ei=qZMfU6mQCsOn-AP89YHoAg"><span class="yt-uix-button-icon-wrapper"><img class="yt-uix-button-icon yt-uix-button-icon-play-all" src="http://s.ytimg.com/yts/img/pixel-vfl3z5WfW.gif" alt="" title="" /></span><span class="yt-uix-button-content">Play </span></a> </h2> 
              <div class="shelf-description yt-ui-ellipsis yt-ui-ellipsis-2">
                The Barbara &amp; Art Culver Center of the Arts grand opening will be preceded by two days of public festivities in Culver Center that will showcase the building, the premi&egrave;re art installations, performances and films.

    <div id="main"> 
     <p> <img src="/research/images/main_images/agricultural_main.jpg" alt="Agricultural Main Image" width="484" height="180" /> </p> 
     <h3>Citrus Experiment Station Gave UCR its Start</h3> 
     <p> Two cottages and a stable on the east side of Mt. Rubidoux comprised the entire station when it opened in 1907 as part of the statewide Agricultural Experiment Station developed by the University of California. </p> 
     <p> Within 10 years, the station had moved to the base of the Box Springs Mountains, where UC Riverside eventually was launched in 1960. The station now is part of the <a href="http://www.cnas.ucr.edu/">College of Natural and Agricultural Sciences</a>, which was organized according to its existing structure in 1974. </p> 
     <h3>Agricultural Experiment Station Offers Real-world Conditions</h3> 
     <p> The <a href="http://agops.ucr.edu/home.html">Agricultural Experiment Station</a> features nearly 1,000 acres of open-air laboratories allow plant scientists to test in real-life conditions everything from how to combat insects and disease to methods for increasing crop productivity. </p> 
     <div class="figure_R" style="width: 221px"> 
      <img src="/research/images/agricultural_citrus.jpg" alt="Citrus Experiment Station" width="217" height="166" /> 
      <p> The Citrus Experiment Station. </p> 
     </div> 
     <p> A 420-acre research center devoted to citrus is located on campus. About 80 miles away in the desert, the 540-acre Coachella Valley Agricultural Research Station offers another field setting in which to test theories on new plant varieties and sustainable agricultural methods. </p> 
     <p> More than 50 different kinds of crops are grown each year for research purposes, from citrus to turf grass to ornamental trees and shrubs. </p> 
    </div> 
    <!-- End Content Area -->

    <h1><a href="/">UC RIVERSIDE PRESENTS</a></h1> 
    <h2>VOICES OF CHANGE: A free series dedicated to the lively exploration of art, artist, and self, one event at a time.</h2> 
   </div> 
   <div id="header-shadow"></div> 
  </div> 
  <!-- end #header --> 
  <div id="posts" class="autopagerize_page_element"> 
   <div class="post"> 
    <div class="date"> 
     <a href="/day/2013/02/01" class="permalink"> <span class="month">Feb</span> <span class="day">01</span> </a> 
    </div> 
    <!-- end .date --> 
    <div class="text"> 
     <h3>David Wax Museum - March 7, 8pm </h3> 
     <div class="text-body"> 
      <p class="MsoNormal"><span>David Wax Museum’s sound tests the boundaries of easy categorization. Singer and guitarist <strong>David Wax</strong> and bandmate <strong>Suz Slezak</strong> (vocals and violin) have cultivated a Mexo-American aesthetic by fusing their knowledge of Mexican folk music with American roots and indie rock. The two crafted their unique sound in and around Boston clubs and in rural Veracruz, Mexico when Wax received a graduate fellowship to study regional musical styles including <em>son jarocho</em>. Slezak, who sings lead, also takes turns playing a fiddle and a traditional Mexican instrument called a <em>guijada</em>, which is fashioned from the jawbone of a donkey. The result is an irrepressible combination of harmonies, Mexican rhythms, and rootsy sound that has become an artistic triumph, earning the winsome duo a spot at the </span><span>prestigious Newport Folk Festival and the 2010 Boston Music Award for Best Americana Artist. Learn more: www.</span><span> <a href="http://www.davidwaxmuseum.com/"></a><a href="http://www.davidwaxmuseum.com/">http://www.davidwaxmuseum.com/</a></span><span></span></p> 
      <p><img alt="David Wax Museum" height="1500" src="http://www.davidwaxmuseum.com/wordpress/wp-content/gallery/shorefire/dwm_tr-34_20120618_151757.jpg" width="1000" /><span>March 7, 2013, 8&nbsp;pm<br /><a href="http://www.culvercenter.ucr.edu/" title="Culver Center of the Arts">Culver Center of the Arts</a><br /> Free </span></p> 
      <p><span><a href="http://maps.google.com/maps?hl=en&amp;gl=us&amp;daddr=3834+Main+Street,+Riverside,+CA+92501&amp;panel=1&amp;f=d&amp;fb=1&amp;dirflg=d&amp;geocode=0,33.981264,-117.374450&amp;cid=0,0,875492350631520353&amp;hq=culver+center+of+the+arts&amp;hnear=0x80dca6df7ff47dbb:0xf7a1d705135e0ae8,Riverside,+CA&amp;sa=X&amp;ei=6FB0UPr_NsjRiAL_xoCICA&amp;ved=0CHUQngIwAA%20" title="map view">map</a></span></p> 
     </div> 
    </div> 
    <!-- end .text -->
